Each priority level is served by a QueueSet that dispatches requests according to virtual time fairness, ensuring that under congestion, all active queues make progress proportionally to their configured concurrency weights. This document traces the architectural boundaries, data flow, algorithmic mechanics, operational tradeoffs, and extension points of this subsystem.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Subsystem Purpose, Boundaries, and Dependencies\n\n### 1.1 Purpose\n\nThe APF QueueSet subsystem enforces request fairness and priority isolation at the API server level by:\n\n1. **Queuing requests** when they arrive faster than the server can serve them\n2. **Dispatching requests fairly** using weighted fair queuing adapted for server requests (where multiple requests can execute concurrently and work duration is unknown until completion)\n3. **Isolating priority levels** so that high-priority flows cannot starve low-priority flows\n4. **Handling work heterogeneity** by estimating per-request \"width\" (seats) to account for different computational costs\n\n### 1.2 Architectural Boundaries\n\n**Upstream Dependencies:**\n- **HTTP Request Pipeline** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/apf_filter.go:155-198`): The APF filter intercepts incoming requests, performs flow classification, and invokes the QueueSet\n- **FlowSchema and PriorityLevelConfiguration API objects**: These control-plane objects define request routing policies and resource allocations\n- **Work Estimator** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/request/width.go:72-136`): Estimates request work based on request type (list, watch, mutating operations)\n- **Authentication/Authorization**: Runs after APF in the request pipeline\n\n**Downstream Components:**\n- **QueueSet**: The core queuing and dispatching engine per priority level\n- **Shuffle Sharding** (`k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/shufflesharding`): Distributes requests across queue selections\n- **Metrics/Observability** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/metrics/`): Tracks concurrency, queue lengths, wait times\n- **Watch Tracker** and **MaxSeatsTracker**: Support watch request initialization signaling and per-priority-level seat limits\n\n### 1.3 Configuration Management\n\nThe `configController` (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/apf_controller.go:99-194`) manages two types of configuration objects:\n\n1. **FlowSchemas**: Define matching criteria (subjects, resources, verbs, non-resource URLs) to classify requests into flows\n2. **PriorityLevelConfigurations**: Define resource allocations (concurrency limits, queue parameters) for each priority level\n\nThe controller maintains eventual consistency with these API objects through informer-based event handlers and a work queue for reprocessing on configuration changes.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Key Components and Responsibility Partition\n\n### 2.1 Core Component Hierarchy\n\n```\nconfigController (apf_controller.go)\n├── priorityLevelState (one per PriorityLevelConfiguration)\n│   ├── QueueSet (queueset.go - the main engine)\n│   │   ├── queue[] (virtual time queuing structures)\n│   │   │   ├── requestsWaiting (FIFO linked list)\n│   │   │   └── requestsExecuting (set tracking concurrent requests)\n│   │   ├── currentR (global progress meter / virtual time)\n│   │   ├── Integrator (seat demand statistics)\n│   │   └── Dealer (shuffle sharding for queue selection)\n│   ├── seatDemandStats (for borrowing decisions)\n│   └── Metrics (concurrency and seat gauges)\n└── flowSchemas[] (sorted by matching precedence)\n```\n\n### 2.2 Request Lifecycle Components\n\n| Component | Location | Responsibility |\n|-----------|----------|-----------------|\n| **APF Filter** | `apf_filter.go:155-198` | HTTP middleware; invokes Handle() on each incoming request |\n| **Request Digest** | `apf_controller.go:110-114` | Lightweight request metadata (user, request info) for classification |\n| **Rule Matcher** | `rule.go:28-149` | FlowSchema matching logic; extracts user, resource rules, non-resource rules |\n| **Work Estimator** | `request/width.go:72-136` | Estimates InitialSeats and FinalSeats based on request type |\n| **request struct** | `queueset/types.go:31-83` | Tracks request state through queuing and execution (arrival time, virtual time, queue position) |\n| **queue struct** | `queueset/types.go:91-110` | Per-queue state: FIFO waiting, virtual start time, executing requests |\n\n### 2.3 Virtual Time and Fairness Components\n\n| Component | Location | Responsibility |\n|-----------|----------|-----------------|\n| **currentR (progress meter)** | `queueset.go:119` | Global virtual time counter; advances as requests execute |\n| **nextDispatchR (queue virtual start)** | `queueset/types.go:97-99` | Virtual start time for requests in each queue; enables per-queue virtual finish time calculation |\n| **arrivalR (request virtual time)** | `queueset/types.go:74-76` | Virtual time at which request arrived; used for virtual finish calculation |\n| **totalWork (request work estimate)** | `queueset/types.go:86-88` | Total work in seat-seconds: (initialSeats × estimatedServiceDuration) + (finalSeats × additionalLatency) |\n\n### 2.4 Concurrency Allocation Components\n\n| Component | Location | Responsibility |\n|-----------|----------|-----------------|\n| **nominalCL** | `apf_controller.go:242-243` | Configured concurrency limit for a priority level |\n| **currentCL** | `apf_controller.go:251-252` | Dynamically adjusted concurrency limit (with borrowing) |\n| **minCL, maxCL** | `apf_controller.go:245-249` | Lower and upper bounds for borrowing adjustments |\n| **seatDemandIntegrator** | `apf_controller.go:230` | Tracks time-weighted seat demand (avg, std dev, high watermark) |\n| **computeConcurrencyAllocation** | `conc_alloc.go:119-257` | Solves fair allocation problem: distributes server concurrency among priority levels respecting bounds and fairness |\n\n---\n\n## 3. End-to-End Control and Request Flow\n\n### 3.1 Configuration Initialization and Update Flow\n\n```\n1. Controller starts → lockAndDigestConfigObjects() [apf_controller.go ~300]\n   ├─ Read all FlowSchema objects, sort by increasing numerical precedence\n   ├─ Read all PriorityLevelConfiguration objects\n   └─ For each PriorityLevel:\n      ├─ Create Integrator for seat demand\n      ├─ Create Metrics (RatioedGaugePair for requests, RatioedGauge for seats)\n      └─ Invoke QueueSetFactory.BeginConstruction() → QueueSetCompleter.Complete()\n         → Create queueSet with initial queue count (DesiredNumQueues)\n\n2. Informer event (FlowSchema or PriorityLevelConfiguration change)\n   └─ configQueue.Add(0) → trigger reprocessing\n\n3. Worker loop processes config queue\n   └─ lockAndDigestConfigObjects() with new objects\n      ├─ BeginConfigChange() on existing QueueSet if reconfiguring\n      └─ Call Complete() with new DispatchingConfig (updated concurrency limits)\n```\n\n**Key File:** `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/apf_controller.go:277-360`\n\n### 3.2 Request Arrival and Classification Flow\n\n```\nREQUEST ARRIVES\n    ↓\napf_filter.Handle() [apf_filter.go:155-198]\n    ├─ Extract RequestDigest (user, requestInfo)\n    ├─ Iterate flowSchemas in order (by precedence)\n    │  └─ Call matchesFlowSchema() [rule.go:30-37]\n    │     └─ For each PolicyRule in FlowSchema.Spec.Rules:\n    │        ├─ matchesASubject() - user/group/service account matching\n    │        └─ matchesResourceRule() or matchesANonResourceRule()\n    │           └─ Check verbs, resources, API groups, namespaces\n    │\n    ├─ On first match: extract PriorityLevelConfiguration name\n    │\n    ├─ Call workEstimator() [request/width.go:107-136]\n    │  ├─ For LIST requests: listWorkEstimator estimates by object count\n    │  ├─ For WATCH requests: if WatchList feature enabled, use listWorkEstimator\n    │  ├─ For CREATE/UPDATE/PATCH/DELETE: mutatingWorkEstimator estimates by watcher count\n    │  └─ Otherwise: return MinimumSeats (1 seat by default)\n    │\n    └─ Call QueueSet.StartRequest() [queueset.go:308-356]\n```\n\n**Key Files:**\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/apf_filter.go:155-203`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/rule.go:28-149`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/request/width.go:107-136`\n\n### 3.3 Queuing and Virtual Time Fairness Flow\n\n```\nQueueSet.StartRequest() [queueset.go:308-356]\n    ├─ STEP 0: If DesiredNumQueues < 1 (no queuing, concurrency-limit-only)\n    │  ├─ Check if request seats can fit in remaining concurrency limit\n    │  ├─ If NO → reject; metrics.AddReject(..., \"concurrency-limit\")\n    │  └─ If YES → dispatchSansQueueLocked() - execute immediately\n    │\n    ├─ STEP 1: Shuffle sharding and enqueuing\n    │  ├─ shuffleShardLocked(hashValue) [queueset.go:583-612]\n    │  │  ├─ Use Dealer.DealIntoHand(hashValue) to select candidate queues\n    │  │  ├─ Pick offset = enqueues % handSize (round-robin across hand)\n    │  │  └─ Select queue with minimum total work (TotalWorkSum)\n    │  │\n    │  └─ shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked() [queueset.go:552-579]\n    │     ├─ Create request struct with arrivalR = currentR (current virtual time)\n    │     ├─ Check if request must be rejected:\n    │     │  └─ (totSeatsInUse >= ConcurrencyLimit) AND (queue.Length >= QueueLengthLimit)\n    │     └─ If OK → enqueueToBoundLocked() [queueset.go:632-651]\n    │        ├─ If queue was empty: set queue.nextDispatchR = currentR\n    │        ├─ Add request to queue.requestsWaiting (FIFO)\n    │        ├─ Update metrics\n    │        └─ Create removal function for the request\n    │\n    ├─ STEP 2: Dispatch as much as possible\n    │  └─ dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked() [queueset.go:653-657]\n    │     └─ While (requests waiting) AND (seats < limit):\n    │        └─ dispatchLocked() [queueset.go:695-743]\n    │           ├─ findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked() [queueset.go:776-822]\n    │           │  ├─ Round-robin through queues\n    │           │  └─ Select queue with minimum (nextDispatchR + oldestRequest.totalWork)\n    │           │     = minimum virtual finish time\n    │           │\n    │           └─ Execute selected request:\n    │              ├─ Remove from queue.requestsWaiting\n    │              ├─ Add to queue.requestsExecuting\n    │              ├─ Update queue.nextDispatchR += request.totalWork()\n    │              └─ Signal promise.Set(decisionExecute)\n    │\n    └─ Return request handle to caller\n\nREQUEST EXECUTION AND FINISH\n    ↓\nrequest.Finish(execFn) [queueset.go:381-395]\n    ├─ request.wait() [queueset.go:397-441]\n    │  ├─ Wait on decision promise (blocked until dispatch or timeout)\n    │  ├─ On decisionExecute: return true, execute request\n    │  └─ On decisionCancel (timeout): return false, reject with \"time-out\"\n    │\n    └─ If executed:\n       └─ finishRequestAndDispatchAsMuchAsPossible() [queueset.go ~900]\n          ├─ Remove request from queue.requestsExecuting\n          ├─ Adjust queue.nextDispatchR for actual service time (if different from estimate)\n          └─ dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked() (cascade dispatch to next queued request)\n```\n\n**Key Files:**\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/fairqueuing/queueset/queueset.go:301-356` (StartRequest)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/fairqueuing/queueset/queueset.go:583-612` (shuffleShardLocked)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/fairqueuing/queueset/queueset.go:695-743` (dispatchLocked)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/fairqueuing/queueset/queueset.go:776-822` (findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked)\n\n### 3.4 Virtual Time Advancement\n\nAt each request arrival, the queueSet synchronizes virtual time:\n\n```\nlockAndSyncTime(ctx) [queueset.go:456-459]\n    └─ syncTimeLocked(ctx) [queueset.go:465-479]\n       ├─ timeSinceLast = clock.Now() - lastRealTime\n       ├─ incrR = SeatsTimesDuration(getVirtualTimeRatio(), timeSinceLast)\n       │  where virtualTimeRatio = min(C, sum(executing_seats)) / activeQueues\n       │                         = min(C, sum of request widths currently executing) / count(non-empty queues)\n       │\n       ├─ currentR += incrR\n       │\n       └─ If currentR >= highR (overflow check):\n          └─ advanceEpoch() [queueset.go:492-522]\n             ├─ Subtract rDecrement from currentR and all queue/request R values\n             └─ Emit metrics.AddEpochAdvance() for overflow tracking\n```\n\n**Key Insight:** Virtual time advances proportionally to the number of active seats relative to the number of active queues. If all C seats are occupied and all queues are active, virtual time advances at rate C nanoseconds per real nanosecond. If fewer seats or queues are active, time advances proportionally slower.\n\n**Key File:** `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/fairqueuing/queueset/queueset.go:461-522`\n\n---\n\n## 4. Failure Modes, Limits, and Design Tradeoffs\n\n### 4.1 Failure Modes\n\n#### Request Rejection Paths\n\n1. **Concurrency Limit Exceeded** (`canAccommodateSeatsLocked()` [queueset.go:748-769])\n   - Condition: `totSeatsInUse + requestSeats > ConcurrencyLimit`\n   - Exception: If total executing requests == 0, allow a single request even if > limit (allows single fat request)\n   - Metric: `metrics.AddReject(..., \"concurrency-limit\")`\n\n2. **Queue Length and Concurrency Both at Limit** (`rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked()` [queueset.go:614-629])\n   - Condition: `(totSeatsInUse >= ConcurrencyLimit) AND (queue.Length >= QueueLengthLimit)`\n   - Reason: Cannot enqueue and cannot execute due to both limits\n   - Metric: `metrics.AddReject(..., \"queue-full\")`\n\n3. **Request Timeout While Queued** (`request.wait()` [queueset.go:397-441])\n   - Condition: Context.Cancel() or context deadline exceeded before dispatch\n   - Action: Remove from queue, decrement wait/seat counts\n   - Metric: `metrics.AddReject(..., \"time-out\")`, `totRequestsCancelled++`\n\n#### Virtual Time Overflow Protection\n\n- **Problem:** `currentR` is a `SeatSeconds` (float64) that grows indefinitely\n- **Solution:** `advanceEpoch()` [queueset.go:492-522] subtracts `rDecrement` (MaxSeatSeconds / 2) when `currentR >= highR`\n- **Safety:** All queue `nextDispatchR` and request `arrivalR` values are decremented correspondingly\n- **Metric:** `metrics.AddEpochAdvance(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, success)` logs overflow count\n\n### 4.2 Design Tradeoffs\n\n#### Virtual Time Ratio Calculation (getVirtualTimeRatioLocked) [queueset.go:526-541]\n\n**Tradeoff:** Using sum of seat demands across all queues vs. per-queue calculation\n\n```go\n// Current implementation\nseatsRequested += (queue.seatsInUse + queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum().MaxSeatsSum)\nreturn min(C, seatsRequested) / activeQueues\n```\n\n**Why:** Ensures fair-queuing fairness across queues based on actual work intensity. A queue with requests requiring many seats (e.g., large list operations) advances its virtual time slower if there are competing queues.\n\n**Tradeoff Impact:**\n- **Pro:** Favors queues with light requests over queues with heavy requests\n- **Con:** Adds per-request work estimate dependency; inaccurate estimates degrade fairness\n\n#### Shuffle Sharding Parameters (HandSize) [queueset.go:583-612]\n\n**Tradeoff:** Randomness vs. queue selection quality\n\n```go\nhand := qs.dealer.DealIntoHand(hashValue, backHand[:])  // HandSize candidate queues\noffset := qs.enqueues % len(hand)                        // Round-robin offset\nbestQueueIdx = hand[selected]                            // Minimum work queue\n```\n\n**Why:** Introduces entropy to distribute flows and reduce head-of-line blocking for correlated flows while maintaining fairness through minimum-work selection.\n\n**Tradeoff Impact:**\n- **Pro:** Prevents hash collisions from starving unrelated flows\n- **Con:** Slightly unpredictable queue assignments; requires careful tuning of HandSize\n\n#### Initial Work Estimate vs. Actual Service Duration [queueset.go:131-146]\n\n**Tradeoff:** Dispatch latency vs. long-term fairness\n\n```go\ncompletedWorkEstimate = {\n    totalWork: computeInitialWork(we) + computeFinalWork(we)\n    finalWork: SeatsTimesDuration(FinalSeats, AdditionalLatency)\n}\n```\n\n**Why:** Dispatch decisions use estimated work, but actual service time is unknown. After execution completes, queue.nextDispatchR is adjusted by the actual work delta.\n\n**Tradeoff Impact:**\n- **Pro:** Allows immediate dispatch decisions without blocking on actual timing\n- **Con:** Under- or over-estimation causes transient fairness deviations that are corrected over time\n\n#### Concurrency Limit Allocation Strategy [conc_alloc.go:119-257]\n\n**Tradeoff:** Fair proportion allocation vs. constraint satisfaction\n\nThe `computeConcurrencyAllocation()` function solves:\n```\nMinimize deviation from fairProp × target[i] for each class\nSubject to: lowerBound[i] ≤ alloc[i] ≤ upperBound[i]\n           Sum(alloc[i]) = totalConcurrency\n```\n\n**Why:** Allocates concurrency fairly among priority levels while respecting operational constraints (e.g., system-critical priority level has minimum concurrency floor).\n\n**Tradeoff Impact:**\n- **Pro:** Respects both fairness and safety bounds\n- **Con:** Complex algorithm; can be unintuitive when bounds are tight\n\n#### Seat Demand Smoothing (seatDemandSmoothingCoefficient = 0.977) [apf_controller.go:88]\n\n**Tradeoff:** Responsiveness vs. stability of borrowing adjustments\n\n```go\nsmoothed = max(envelope, A*smoothed + (1-A)*envelope)\n           where envelope = avg + stdDev, A = 0.977\n```\n\n**Why:** Reduces thrashing in borrowing decisions; half-life ~5 minutes (initial design guess).\n\n**Tradeoff Impact:**\n- **Pro:** Prevents borrowing oscillations under bursty load\n- **Con:** Slow reaction to sustained demand changes; may under-allocate during ramps\n\n---\n\n## 5. Operational Implications and Observability\n\n### 5.1 Request Lifecycle Metrics\n\nThe subsystem emits comprehensive metrics at each stage:\n\n| Metric | When Emitted | Semantic |\n|--------|-------------|----------|\n| `requests_in_queues` | Enqueue, Dispatch, Reject | Count of requests waiting in queues |\n| `seats_in_queues` | Enqueue, Dispatch, Reject | Total seat-seconds allocated to waiting requests |\n| `requests_executing` | Dispatch, Finish | Count of executing requests |\n| `seat_concurrency_in_use` | Dispatch, Finish | Total seats occupied (real-time) |\n| `seat_demand` | Every sync interval | Time-weighted integral of occupied + queued seats |\n| `waiting_duration` | Dispatch or Reject | Time from arrival to dispatch or rejection |\n| `execution_duration` | Finish | Time from dispatch to completion |\n| `queue_length` | Per-queue snapshot | Requests waiting in each queue |\n| `epoch_advance_total` | Virtual time overflow | Count of R overflow events |\n\n**Key File:** `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/metrics/metrics.go`\n\n### 5.2 Queue State Introspection\n\nThe `Dump()` method [queueset.go:822] snapshots the internal state for debugging:\n\n```go\ntype QueueSetDump struct {\n    Queues     []QueueDump       // Per-queue state\n    Waiting    int               // Total requests waiting\n    Executing  int               // Total requests executing\n    Dispatched int               // Cumulative dispatched count\n    Rejected   int               // Cumulative rejected count\n    Timedout   int               // Cumulative timeout count\n    Cancelled  int               // Cumulative cancel count\n}\n\ntype QueueDump struct {\n    NextDispatchR     string                 // Queue's virtual start time (stringified)\n    Requests          []RequestDump          // Waiting requests with arrival times\n    RequestsExecuting int                    // Count executing from this queue\n    SeatsInUse        int                    // Seats occupied in this queue\n    QueueSum          struct {\n        InitialSeatsSum  int                 // Sum of request initial seats\n        MaxSeatsSum      int                 // Sum of request max seats\n        TotalWorkSum     string               // Total work in seat-seconds\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis is leveraged by the controller's debug endpoints in `apf_controller_debug.go`.\n\n### 5.3 Concurrency Borrowing Behavior\n\nThe `priorityLevelState` maintains `seatDemandStats` [apf_controller.go:255-260] updated periodically (~10 seconds):\n\n```go\nseatDemandStats {\n    avg            // Time-weighted average seats in use\n    stdDev         // Standard deviation\n    highWatermark  // Peak seats observed\n    smoothed       // Exponentially smoothed envelope (avg + stdDev)\n}\n```\n\nPeriodically, the controller invokes `computeConcurrencyAllocation()` to adjust per-level concurrency limits based on smoothed demand, allowing overloaded levels to borrow from idle levels while maintaining global concurrency.\n\n**Operational Insight:** Monitor `seat_demand_ratio` (seat_demand / nominalCL) per priority level:\n- Ratio ~1.0: Level is operating near capacity; may benefit from higher nominalCL or lower queue limits\n- Ratio >> 1.0: Level is heavily borrowing; consider increasing nominalCL or reducing incoming load\n- Ratio << 1.0: Level is underutilized; concurrency may be wasted; consider borrowing rules\n\n---\n\n## 6. Extension Points and Customization Hooks\n\n### 6.1 Work Estimator Customization\n\nThe `WorkEstimator` interface [request/width.go:89] allows custom estimation logic:\n\n```go\ntype WorkEstimatorFunc func(request *http.Request,\n    flowSchemaName, priorityLevelName string) WorkEstimate\n\n// Implementation per verb:\n// - LIST: objectCountFn(resource) → list object count → estimate seats\n// - WATCH: (with WatchList) same as LIST\n// - MUTATING: watchCountFn(requestInfo) → watcher count → estimate seats\n// - Others: minimumSeats (default 1)\n```\n\n**Extension Risk:** Inaccurate estimation → unfair dispatch order; requests with overestimated seats starve those with underestimated seats.\n\n**Mitigation:** Separate `InitialSeats` (dispatch time estimate) and `FinalSeats` (true final resource demand); post-execution adjustment via actual service time.\n\n**Key Files:**\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/request/width.go`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/request/list_work_estimator.go`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/request/mutating_work_estimator.go`\n\n### 6.2 Flow Distinguisher Method\n\nFlowSchema `DistinguisherMethod` [api/flowcontrol/v1] allows custom flow partitioning:\n\n```\nDistinguisherMethod {\n  type: \"ByUser\" | \"ByNamespace\" | \"ByUserAndNamespace\" | ...\n}\n```\n\nThis determines the `hashValue` used in shuffle sharding; different distinguishers route correlated flows to different queues.\n\n**Extension Risk:** Poorly chosen distinguisher → hash collisions → queue imbalance.\n\n### 6.3 Priority Level Configuration\n\n`PriorityLevelConfiguration` allows tuning:\n\n```go\ntype PriorityLevelConfigurationSpec struct {\n    Type: \"Exempt\" | \"Limited\"\n    Limited: {\n        NominalConcurrencyLimit: 100        // Target seats\n        BorrowingLimit: 50                   // Max borrow from pool\n        LendablePercent: 20                  // % available for borrowing\n    }\n    Queuing: {\n        DesiredNumQueues: 16                 // Number of queues\n        QueueLengthLimit: 50                 // Per-queue waiting limit\n        HandSize: 8                          // Shuffle sharding hand size\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Tuning Impacts:**\n- High `DesiredNumQueues` → better isolation, higher memory cost\n- High `HandSize` → lower collision probability, slightly slower queue selection\n- High `QueueLengthLimit` → more buffering, higher rejection latency variability\n\n### 6.4 Promise Factory (Testing Hook)\n\nThe `promiseFactory` [queueset.go:44, 361-362] allows injection of custom promise implementations for testing:\n\n```go\ntype promiseFactory func(initial interface{}, doneCtx context.Context, doneVal interface{}) promise.WriteOnce\n\n// Ordinaryimplementation uses promise.NewWriteOnce, a simple write-once pattern\n// Tests can inject mock implementations to simulate timeouts, race conditions, etc.\n```\n\n**Key File:** `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/fairqueuing/promise/`\n\n---\n\n## 7. Algorithmic Fairness Guarantees and Tradeoffs\n\n### 8.1 Fair Queuing Bound\n\nTraditional fair queuing provides: _divergence from ideal ≤ 1 packet_\n\nAdapted for concurrent requests: _divergence from ideal ≤ C requests_\n\n**Meaning:** Under virtual time fairness, the actual service received by queue i can diverge from its fair share by at most C request executions. This bound degrades gracefully under:\n- High concurrency limits (C is large)\n- Long-running requests (single request dominates dispatch time)\n\n### 8.2 Virtual Time Computation\n\nKey formula [queueset.go:526-541]:\n\n```\nvirtualTimeRate = min(C, sum(active_request_seats)) / activeQueues\ncurrentR += virtualTimeRate × realTimeDelta\n```\n\n**Fairness Property:**\n- If all C seats are full and N queues are active, each queue advances at rate C/N nanoseconds/real-nanosecond\n- Virtual start times ensure that queues with less work get priority for dispatch\n- Round-robin selection among tied minimum virtual finish times provides FIFO fairness within a queue\n\n### 8.3 Entropy Introduction via Shuffle Sharding\n\nDespite deterministic queue selection (minimum work), shuffle sharding's randomness [queueset.go:583-612] ensures:\n\n1. **Hash collision reduction:** Different flows map to different queues probabilistically\n2. **Correlated request isolation:** Related requests don't all go to the same queue\n3. **Bounded latency variance:** Worst-case queue length is O(total_queue_length / num_queues)\n\n**Tradeoff:** Determinism (reproducibility) vs. robustness (no worst-case collision patterns).\n\n---\n\n## 9. Summary of Critical Implementation Details\n\n### 9.1 Lock Ordering and Concurrency Safety\n\nAll mutable QueueSet state is guarded by `qs.lock` (sync.Mutex) [queueset.go:97]:\n\n```\nMethods acquiring lock:\n  - lockAndSyncTime() - Always called before modifying queue state\n  - IsIdle()\n  - Dump()\n\nMethods assuming lock is held:\n  - *Locked suffix: syncTimeLocked, dispatchLocked, etc.\n\nLock lifecycle:\n  - Held during entire StartRequest() call\n  - Released during request.wait() and execFn() execution\n  - Re-acquired in request.Finish() to update state\n```\n\n**Safety:** No concurrent dispatch or virtual time updates to the same queueset.\n\n### 9.2 Virtual Time Invariants\n\n1. **Monotonicity:** `currentR` never decreases (except advanceEpoch subtracts uniformly)\n2. **Queue ordering:** If queue A has fewer waiting requests than queue B, and both arrive at same time, queue A's nextDispatchR ≤ queue B's nextDispatchR\n3. **Progress:** currentR increases as long as there are executing requests or waiting requests with active queues\n\n### 9.3 Request Lifecycle State Machine\n\n```\nRequest Lifecycle:\n  CREATED → ENQUEUED → DECIDED → EXECUTED/REJECTED\n\nStates:\n  - decision promise: nil → decisionExecute | decisionCancel\n  - queue position: in waitingList → in executingSet | removed\n  - startTime: unset until dispatch\n  - waitStarted flag: prevents double-wait\n\nEdge cases:\n  - Request never waited on (filtered/rejected before startRequest returns)\n  - Request cancelled between enqueue and dispatch (decision = decisionCancel)\n  - Request times out in queue (wait() receives decisionCancel on timeout)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Key Performance Considerations\n\n### 10.1 Dispatch Selection Cost\n\n`findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked()` [queueset.go:776-822] is O(num_queues):\n\n```go\nfor range qs.queues {                    // O(num_queues)\n    queue := qs.queues[qs.robinIndex]\n    currentVirtualFinish := queue.nextDispatchR + oldestWaiting.totalWork()\n    if currentVirtualFinish < minVirtualFinish {\n        minVirtualFinish = currentVirtualFinish\n        minQueue = queue\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Impact:** With many queues, dispatch becomes a bottleneck. Typical deployments use O(10-100) queues per priority level.\n\n### 10.2 Shuffle Sharding Cost\n\nDealer.DealIntoHand() [external] is O(HandSize) per request, where HandSize is typically 8.\n\n**Impact:** Negligible compared to dispatch selection.\n\n### 10.3 Memory Footprint\n\nPer QueueSet:\n- **Queues:** DesiredNumQueues × (waitingList + executingSet) → O(DesiredNumQueues × QueueLengthLimit)\n- **Metrics:** RatioedGaugePair + RatioedGauge + Integrator → O(1) per priority level\n- **Virtual time tracking:** O(num_executing_requests) for tracking actualwork\n\n**Typical:** 1-10 MB per QueueSet under load.\n\n---\n\n## 11. Conclusion\n\nThe APF QueueSet subsystem provides **weighted fair queuing** for Kubernetes API server requests through:\n\n1. **Virtual time fairness:** Queue progress proportional to concurrency weight, isolated from real-time variations\n2. **Adaptive queuing:** Shuffle sharding reduces hash collisions; per-queue management enables fine-grained flow control\n3. **Work heterogeneity:** Seat-based estimates accommodate diverse request costs (list vs. simple get)\n4. **Borrowing:** Dynamic concurrency allocation respects priority levels while allowing oversubscribed workloads\n5. **Observability:** Comprehensive metrics and dump endpoints enable operational debugging\n\nThe implementation balances **algorithmic correctness** (fair queuing bounds, virtual time monotonicity) with **operational pragmatism** (grace under overload, efficient dispatch, customization hooks).\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
